### ä¸»è¦æ–°åŠŸèƒ½
- **å…¨é¢æ”¯æŒ [Manticore Columnar Library](https://github.com/manticoresoftware/columnar)**ã€‚æ­¤å‰ Manticore Columnar Library ä»…æ”¯æŒæ™®é€šç´¢å¼•ã€‚ç°åœ¨æ”¯æŒï¼š

